рдЖрд╡реГрддреНрддрд┐-рд░рд╛рд╣рд┐рддреНрдпрдореН

рдиреАрд▓рдореЗрдШрдГ (рд╕рдВ)

тАШтАШрд╕рдХреГрддреН рдХреГрддрд╢реН рд╢рд╛рд╕реНрддреНрд░рд╛рд░реНрдердГтАЩтАЩ()

рдЗрддрд┐ рдирд┐рд░реНрдгрдпрд╕реНрдп,
+++(рдЖрд╡реГрддреНрддрд┐-рд╡рд┐рдзрд┐-рд╕рд╣рд┐рддтЖТ)+++ рдЙрдкрд╛рд╕рдиреЗ рдЗрд╡рд╛рддреНрд░ рдЖрд╡реГрддреНрддрд┐-рдкрд░реЛ рд╜рдкрд╡рд╛рджреЛ рдирд╛рд╕реНрддрд┐ ред

English

There is a ( well-known) principle which states:

тАЬWhen an action is enjoined in the ┼Ы─Бstra,
a single performance of it satisfies the requirements of the ┼Ъ─Бstra”.

The up─Бsana however, is an exception to this general rule
because it requires frequent repetition.
But prapatti is no such exception
(and hence a single performance will quite do ).

Espa├▒ol

Hay existe un principio (bien conocido) que establece:

тАЬCuando se prescribe una acci├│n en el ┼Ы─Бstra,
una sola ejecuci├│n del mismo satisface los requisitos del ┼Ъ─Бstra".

El up─Бsana, sin embargo, es una excepci├│n a esta regla general
porque requiere repetici├│n frecuente.
Pero prapatti no es tal excepci├│n
(y por lo tanto una sola actuaci├│n ser├б suficiente).

English

This statement is confirmed also by such words as the following: -

“To the man who performs prapatti only once
and says “I exist for Thee " -
to that man I grant freedom from fear
from all beings.
This is my vow”.

Espa├▒ol

“Para el hombre que realiza prapatti s├│lo una vez
y dice “Yo existo para Ti” -
A ese hombre le concedo libertad del miedo.
de todos los seres.
Este es mi voto”.

рдиреАрд▓рдореЗрдШрдГ (рд╕рдВ)

(рдПрд╡рдВ) рдорд╣реЛрджрд╛рд░рд╕реНрдп рд╕рд░реНрд╡рд╢рдХреНрддреЗрдГ рд╕рдиреНрдирд┐рдзреМ

English

To the man who performs bharany─Бsa (the surrender of responsibility) to the generous and omnipotent (Lord),
there is no reason for delay in the attainment
except his own desire.

Espa├▒ol

no hay ninguna raz├│n para retraso en el logro
excepto su propio deseo.

рдиреАрд▓рдореЗрдШрдГ (рд╕рдВ)

“рд╕рд░реНрд╡рд╛рддреНрдо-рдирд┐рдпрдиреНрддреИрдХреЛ рд╜рд╕реНрддреА"рддреНрдпреН рдЕрд╕реНрдпрд╛рд░реНрдерд╕реНрдпрд╛рд╕рд┐рджреНрдзреНрдпрд╛

English

If (on the other hand) it be maintained that the j─лva’s doership is dependent only on himself (and on nobody else),
then since it would resemble the heresy which does not admit the existence of one who is in supreme control of all selves,
it would be a form of atheism.

entonces, dado que se parecer├нa a la herej├нa que no admite la existencia de alguien que est├б en control supremo de todos los seres,
ser├нa una forma de ate├нsmo.

If it is held that the doership which comes from the will of the Lord is merely the state of being the knower,
there would be no such thing as a desire for the ends of life (puruс╣г─Бrtha)

y el esfuerzo de alcanzarlos.

English

The doership or agentship which consists in being the seat (─Б┼Ыraya) of an action
(or the place where an action takes place)
is a common attribute of both sentient beings and non sentient things
(for the latter also move about and undergo changes).

But the seat (─Б┼Ыraya) of an effort or endeavour (prayatna) is (an attribute) peculiar to sentient beings.

Espa├▒ol

El agencia que consiste en ser la sede (─Б┼Ыraya) de una acci├│n
(o el lugar donde tiene lugar una acci├│n)
es un atributo com├║n tanto de los seres sintientes como de las cosas no sintientes
(para este ├║ltimo tambi├йn moverse y sufrir cambios).

Pero la sede (─Б┼Ыraya) de un esfuerzo o empe├▒o (prayatna) es (un atributo) peculiar de los seres sintientes.

English

If it be asked how this could be understood,
the answer is as follows:-

The texts which declare that the self is not a doer or agent
have, for their purport, the truth that
the doership of the self which is dependent on I┼Ыvara and on the qualities of prakс╣Ыti (sattva, rajas and tamas)
should not be considered as independent of other (forms).

Espa├▒ol

Si se pregunta c├│mo podr├нa entenderse esto,
la respuesta es la siguiente:-

Los textos que declaran que el yo no es un hacedor o agente
tienen, a su entender, la verdad de que
la hacedor del yo que depende de I┼Ыvara y de las cualidades de prakс╣Ыti (sattva, rajas y tamas)
no debe considerarse como independiente de otras (formas).

English

as stated in the ┼Ыloka:

“The four castes were created by me
in accordance with such qualities as sattva
that are found in j─лvas
and also with their past karma .
Though I perform the act of creation,
I am not the real cause
nor am I tainted by it.”

Espa├▒ol

como indica en el ┼Ыloka:

“Las cuatro castas fueron creadas por m├н
de acuerdo con cualidades tales como sattva
que se encuentran en j─лvas
y tambi├йn con su karma pasado.
Aunque realizo el acto de creaci├│n,
Yo no soy la verdadera causa
ni estoy contaminado por eso.”

English

Thus from I┼Ыvara who has the common and general doership of all things without exception,
the j─лva acquires the power to make an effort and act in accordance with his own will.

Therefore it is evident that
the j─лva is fit to be directed to do a thing
and the word “vraja” may justly enjoin the performance of an action.

Espa├▒ol

As├н, de I┼Ыvara quien tiene la autor├нa com├║n y general de todas las cosas sin excepci├│n,
la j─лva adquiere el poder de hacer un esfuerzo y actuar de acuerdo con su propia voluntad.

Por lo tanto es evidente que
la j─лva es apta para ser dirigida a hacer una cosa
y la palabra “vraja” puede justamente prohibir la realizaci├│n de una acci├│n.

English

Bhakti as an up─Бya has been compared (by some critics of it)
to “water from a sacred river
contained in a pitcher
but mingled with a drop of liquor”.

But this comparison or simile would hold good
only when egoism is mingled with (bhakti ).
The same condemnation would hold good in the case of prapatti also,
when it is mingled with egoism or ahank─Бra.

Espa├▒ol

Bhakti como up─Бya ha sido comparado (por algunos cr├нticos)
al “agua de un r├нo sagrado
contenido en una jarra
pero mezclado con una gota de licor”.

Pero esta comparaci├│n o s├нmil ser├нa v├бlida
s├│lo cuando el ego├нsmo se mezcla con (bhakti).

La misma condena ser├нa v├бlida tambi├йn en el caso de prapatti,
cuando est├б mezclado con ego├нsmo o ahank─Бra.

English

It is stated by some that
Aс╕╖avand─Бr begs forgiveness for having performed prapatti.

Here Aс╕╖avand─Бr is seeking pardon for any trace af egoism (ahaс╣Еk─Бra) that might have been present in him
and no more than that.

Espa├▒ol

Algunos afirman que
Aс╕╖avand─Бr pide perd├│n por haber realizado prapatti.

Aqu├н Aс╕╖avand─Бr est├б buscando perd├│n por cualquier rastro de ego├нsmo (ahaс╣Еk─Бra) que podr├нa haber estado presente en ├йl

рдиреАрд▓рдореЗрдШрдГ (рд╕рдВ)

рдЗрддреНрдердВ рдкрд░рд╛рдзреАрди-рдХрд░реНрддреГрддреНрд╡рд╕реНрдп рдкреНрд░рд╛рдорд╛рдгрд┐рдХрддреНрд╡рд╛рддреН,

‘рдЖрддреНрдордирдГ рдХрд░реНрддреГрддреНрд╡рд╛рднрд╛рд╡рд╛рддреН

рдЗрддрд┐ рдкрдХреНрд╖реЛ рд╜рдкрд┐ рдирд┐рд░рд╕реНрддрдГ ред

English

There is a (wrong ) view that

the self has no real doership
and therefore if a man knows this real nature of his (that he is not a doer),
none of the forbidden actions that might be performed by him
will leave any stain on him.

Since the doership of the j─лva is subject (to the will of I┼Ыvara ),
This view finds its refutation
(also in what has been said so far.)
[Commentary fixed.]

Espa├▒ol

Hay una vista (incorrecta) que

el yo no tiene agencia real
y por lo tanto, si un hombre conoce esta verdadera naturaleza suya (que no es un hacedor),
ninguna de las acciones prohibidas que podr├нa realizar ├йl
dejar├б cualquier mancha en ├йl.

Dado que la agencia de la j─лva est├б sujeto (a la voluntad de I┼Ыvara),

“To those that have not renounced their doership and the fruit of their actions,
the fruits of their karma will (certainly) follow

qu├й es indeseable, qu├й es deseable y qu├й es en parte deseable y en parte indeseable.

" He who, while performing an action, does not think that

" When there is a real fear

English

“At a time when there is a fear that
want of food might cause death,
the man that eats the food obtained by him,
whatever the source might be,
will not be stained by the sin thereof,
in the same way as water does not wet the leaf of the lotus.”

(They) prescribed the conditions under which
transgressions may be permitted.

That this rule applies equally to the man who knows or meditates on Brahman
is seen stated in the S┼лtra which says,

“At a time when death is feared ( owing to starvation ),
the man (the man who meditates on Brahman) may eat any food, whatsoever,
for the ┼Ы─Бstras say so тАЭ

and this is taught there with the help of an illustration.

(ILLUSTRATION.
Ushasti was a seer
and when owing to starvation, he feared he might die,
he ate the cooked grain given to him by a man of a low caste.

he refused what was offered to him afterwards viz. water.)

English

“I am the means
as well as the end to be attained.
The aspirant (to mukti) should become subject to me
and seek my protection.
The up─Бya called ┼Ыaraс╣З─Бgati is not the direct means for the attainment.
Sadhanas or means like bhakti yoga and karma yoga are no aids to prapatti;
other troublesome aс╣Еgas are not required for prapatti.
I will myself stand in the place of all such means
(as are prescribed for attaining the desired fruits).
I am the messenger and the master.
Seek me as your refuge
and be free from all anxiety”.

So says the Lord
and surrounds me on all sides.

y busca mi protecci├│n.
El up─Бya llamado ┼Ыaraс╣З─Бgati no es el medio directo para el logro.
Sadhanas o medios como bhakti yoga y karma yoga no son ayudas para prapatti;
otros aс╣Еgas problem├бticos no son necesarios para prapatti.
Yo mismo estar├й en el lugar de todos esos medios
(como est├бn prescritos para alcanzar los frutos deseados).
Yo soy el mensajero y el maestro.
B├║scame como tu refugio
y sea libre de toda ansiedad”.

As├н dice el Se├▒or
y me rodea por todos lados.
